iterations).\n\n# Let me check if we can reduce this by using multiple pairs simultaneously.\n# For each pair i, we have:\n# L0_i ^ f(R0p_i ^ K0) = L4_i ^ f(L3_i ^ K2)  where L3_i = R4_i ^ f(L4_i ^ K3)\n# R0p_i ^ f(L0_i ^ f(R0p_i ^ K0) ^ K1) = L3_i = R4_i ^ f(L4_i ^ K3)\n\n# These are 2 equations per pair, with 4 unknowns (K0, K1, K2, K3).\n# With 2 pairs, we have 4 equations and 4 unknowns. Should be solvable!\n\nprint(\"\\nSolving the system with 2 pairs...\")\n\n# Let's use pair 0 and pair 1\npt0, ct0 = pairs[0]\npt1, ct1 = pairs[1]\n\nL0_0 = getleft(pt0)\nR0_0 = getright(pt0)\nR0p_0 = R0_0 ^ L0_0\nR4_0 = getleft(ct0)\nL4_0 = getright(ct0) ^ R4_0\n\nL0_1 = getleft(pt1)\nR0_1 = getright(pt1)\nR0p_1 = R0_1 ^ L0_1\nR4_1 = getleft(ct1)\nL4_1 = getright(ct1) ^ R4_1\n\nprint(f\"Pair 0: L0=0x{L0_0:08X}, R0p=0x{R0p_0:08X}, L4=0x{L4_0:08X}, R4=0x{R4_0:08X}\")\nprint(f\"Pair 1: L0=0x{L0_1:08X}, R0p=0x{R0p_1:08X}, L4=0x{L4_1:08X}, R4=0x{R4_1:08X}\")\n\n# From equations for pair 0:\n# R1_0 = L0_0 ^ f(R0p_0 ^ K0) = L4_0 ^ f(L3_0 ^ K2)  where L3_0 = R4_0 ^ f(L4_0 ^ K3)\n# L3_0 = R0p_0 ^ f(R1_0 ^ K1)\n\n# From equations for pair 1:\n# R1_1 = L0_1 ^ f(R0p_1 ^ K0) = L4_1 ^ f(L3_1 ^ K2)  where L3_1 = R4_1 ^ f(L4_1 ^ K3)\n# L3_1 = R0p_1 ^ f(R1_1 ^ K1)\n\n# Equating R1 expressions:\n# L0_0 ^ f(R0p_0 ^ K0) ^ L4_0 = f(L3_0 ^ K2)\n# L0_1 ^ f(R0p_1 ^ K0) ^ L4_1 = f(L3_1 ^ K2)\n\n# Since K2 is the same in both:\n# f_inv(L0_0 ^ f(R0p_0 ^ K0) ^ L4_0) ^ L3_0 = f_inv(L0_1 ^ f(R0p_1 ^ K0) ^ L4_1) ^ L3_1\n# => L3_0 ^ L3_1 = f_inv(L0_0 ^ f(R0p_0 ^ K0) ^ L4_0) ^ f_inv(L0_1 ^ f(R0p_1 ^ K0) ^ L4_1)\n# => (R4_0 ^ f(L4_0 ^ K3)) ^ (R4_1 ^ f(L4_1 ^ K3)) = f_inv(L0_0 ^ f(R0p_0 ^ K0) ^ L4_0) ^ f_inv(L0_1 ^ f(R0p_1 ^ K0) ^ L4_1)\n\n# This gives us LHS in terms of K3 only, RHS in terms of K0 only!\n# So we can do MITM!\n\nprint(\"\\nBuilding forward hash (K0 -> RHS)...\")\n\n# Compute RHS = f_inv(L0_0 ^ f(R0p_0 ^ K0) ^ L4_0) ^ f_inv(L0_1 ^ f(R0p_1 ^ K0) ^ L4_1)\nforward_table = {}  # RHS -> list of K0 seeds\n\n# But wait, RHS is 32 bits, so many different K0 values could produce the same RHS.\n# For each K0, compute RHS and store in dictionary.\n\nfor k0_seed in range(1<<20):\n    ek0 = expanded[k0_seed]\n    # Compute RHS\n    term0 = f_inverse(L0_0 ^ f_function(R0p_0 ^ ek0) ^ L4_0)\n    term1 = f_inverse(L0_1 ^ f_function(R0p_1 ^ ek0) ^ L4_1)\n    rhs = term0 ^ term1\n    if rhs not in forward_table:\n        forward_table[rhs] = []\n    forward_table[rhs].append(k0_seed)\n    \n    if k0_seed % 100000 == 0:\n        print(f\"  Forward progress: {k0_seed}/{1<<20}\")\n\nprint(f\"Forward table built with {len(forward_table)} unique RHS values\")\n\n# Now iterate over K3 and compute LHS = (R4_0 ^ f(L4_0 ^ K3)) ^ (R4_1 ^ f(L4_1 ^ K3))\n# Look up RHS in forward table.\n\nprint(\"\\nSearching backward (K3 -> match)...\")\nfound = False\nfor k3_seed in range(1<<20):\n    ek3 = expanded[k3_seed]\n    L3_0 = R4_0 ^ f_function(L4_0 ^ ek3)\n    L3_1 = R4_1 ^ f_function(L4_1 ^ ek3)\n    lhs = L3_0 ^ L3_1\n    \n    if lhs in forward_table:\n        print(f\"Found match for K3=0x{k3_seed:05X}\")\n        for k0_seed in forward_table[lhs]:\n            ek0 = expanded[k0_seed]\n            # Now derive K2 and K1\n            # From pair 0: K2 = f_inv(R1_0 ^ L4_0) ^ L3_0\n            R1_0 = L0_0 ^ f_function(R0p_0 ^ ek0)\n            k2_exp = f_inverse(R1_0 ^ L4_0) ^ L3_0\n            \n            # From pair 0: K1 = f_inv(L3_0 ^ R0p_0) ^ R1_0\n            k1_exp = f_inverse(L3_0 ^ R0p_0) ^ R1_0\n            \n            keys = [ek0, k1_exp, k2_exp, ek3]\n            \n            # Verify with all 32 pairs\n            ok = True\n            for pt, ct in pairs:\n                if encrypt(pt, keys) != ct:\n                    ok = False\n                    break\n            \n            if ok:\n                print(f\"\\nFOUND KEYS!\")\n                print(f\"K0_seed=0x{k0_seed:05X}, exp=0x{ek0:08X}\")\n                print(f\"K1_exp=0x{k1_exp:08X}\")\n                print(f\"K2_exp=0x{k2_exp:08X}\")\n                print(f\"K3_seed=0x{k3_seed:05X}, exp=0x{ek3:08X}\")\n                \n                # Find seeds for K1 and K2\n                for s in range(1<<20):\n                    if expanded[s] == k1_exp:\n                        print(f\"K1_seed=0x{s:05X}\")\n                    if expanded[s] == k2_exp:\n                        print(f\"K2_seed=0x{s:05X}\")\n                \n                # Decrypt ciphertexts\n                with open('/app/ciphertexts.txt', 'r') as f:\n                    lines = f.readlines()\n                \n                with open('/app/plaintexts.txt', 'w') as f:\n                    for line in lines:\n                        ct_val = int(line.strip())\n                        left = getright(ct_val)\n                        right = getleft(ct_val)\n                        left ^= right\n                        for r in range(3, -1, -1):\n                            temp = left\n                            left = right\n                            mixed = f_function(temp ^ keys[r])\n                            right = temp\n                            left ^= mixed\n                        right ^= left\n                        pt_val = merge(left, right)\n                        f.write(f\"{pt_val}\\n\")\n                \n                print(f\"\\nDecrypted to /app/plaintexts.txt\")\n                \n                # Verify by checking the binary\n                import subprocess\n                result = subprocess.run(['./decrypt', 'ciphertexts.txt', \n                    f'{k0_seed:05x}', f'{k3_seed:05x}', f'{k3_seed:05x}', f'{k3_seed:05x}'],\n                    capture_output=True, text=True, cwd='/app')\n                print(f\"Binary decryption test: {result.stdout[:100]}\")\n                \n                found = True\n                break\n        if found:\n            break\n    \n    if k3_seed % 100000 == 0:\n        print(f\"  Backward progress: {k3_seed}/{1<<20}\")\n    \n    if found:\n        break\n\nif not found:\n    print(\"Not found!\")\nEOF\ntimeout 60 python3 /app/linear_attack.py 2>&1\n",
      "duration": 0.1
    }
  ],
  "task_complete": false
}
```
